<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">18th century</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">

<div class="thumb tright">

<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Canadian_militiamen_and_British_soldiers_repulse_the_American_assault_at_Sault-au-Matelot.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a href="/wiki/American_Revolutionary_War" title="American Revolutionary War">American Revolutionary War</a> took place in the late 18th century.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <b>18th century</b> lasted from January 1, <a href="/wiki/1701" title="1701">1701</a> to December 31, <a href="/wiki/1800" title="1800">1800</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>. During the 18th century, the <a href="/wiki/Age_of_Enlightenment" title="Age of Enlightenment">Enlightenment</a> culminated in the <a href="/wiki/French_Revolution" title="French Revolution">French</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_revolution" title="American revolution">American revolutions</a>. Philosophy and science increased in prominence. Philosophers dreamed of a brighter age. This dream turned into a reality with the <a href="/wiki/French_Revolution" title="French Revolution">French Revolution</a> of 1789-, though later compromised by the excesses of the <a href="/wiki/Reign_of_Terror" title="Reign of Terror">Reign of Terror</a> (1793–1794) under <a href="/wiki/Maximilien_Robespierre" title="Maximilien Robespierre">Maximilien Robespierre</a>. At first, many monarchies of <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> embraced Enlightenment ideals, but with the French Revolution they feared losing their power and formed broad coalitions for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Counter-revolution" title="Counter-revolution">counter-revolution</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman Empire</a> experienced an unprecedented period of peace and economic expansion, taking part in no European wars from 1740 to 1768. As a consequence the empire did not share in Europe's military improvements during the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Years%27_War" title="Seven Years' War">Seven Years' War</a> (1756–1763), causing its military to fall behind and suffer defeats against <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">Russia</a> in the second half of the century.</p>
<p>The 18th century also marked the end of the <a href="/wiki/Polish%E2%80%93Lithuanian_Commonwealth" title="Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth">Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth</a> as an independent state. The once-powerful and vast kingdom, which had once conquered <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> and defeated great Ottoman armies, collapsed under numerous invasions. Its semi-democratic government system was not robust enough to rival the neighboring monarchies of the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Prussia" title="Kingdom of Prussia">Kingdom of Prussia</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">Russian Empire</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Archduchy_of_Austria" title="Archduchy of Austria">Archduchy of Austria</a> which divided the Commonwealth territories between themselves, changing the landscape of <a href="/wiki/Central_Europe" title="Central Europe">Central European</a> politics for the next hundred years.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/European_colonization_of_the_Americas" title="European colonization of the Americas">European colonization of the Americas</a> and other parts of the world intensified and associated mass migrations of people grew in size as the <a href="/wiki/Age_of_Sail" title="Age of Sail">Age of Sail</a> continued. <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Great Britain</a> became a major power worldwide with the <a href="/wiki/French_and_Indian_War" title="French and Indian War">defeat of France in North America</a> in the 1760s and <a href="/wiki/Company_rule_in_India" title="Company rule in India">the conquest of large parts of India</a>. However, Britain lost many of its North American colonies after the <a href="/wiki/American_Revolution" title="American Revolution">American Revolution</a>, which resulted in the formation of the newly independent <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Industrial_Revolution" title="Industrial Revolution">Industrial Revolution</a> started in Britain in the 1770s with the production of the improved <a href="/wiki/Steam_engine" title="Steam engine">steam engine</a>. Despite its modest beginnings in the 18th century, steam-powered machinery would radically change human society and the environment.</p>
<p>Western historians have occasionally defined the 18th century otherwise for the purposes of their work. For example, the "short" 18th century may be defined as 1715–1789, denoting the period of time between the death of <a href="/wiki/Louis_XIV_of_France" title="Louis XIV of France">Louis XIV of France</a> and the start of the French Revolution, with an emphasis on directly interconnected events.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> To historians who expand the century to include larger historical movements, the "long" 18th century<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Baines_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-Baines-3">[3]</a></sup> may run from the <a href="/wiki/Glorious_Revolution" title="Glorious Revolution">Glorious Revolution</a> of 1688 to the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Waterloo" title="Battle of Waterloo">Battle of Waterloo</a> in <a href="/wiki/1815" title="1815">1815</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> or even later.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

</ul>
</div>
<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1700s"><a href="/wiki/1700s_(decade)" title="1700s (decade)">1700s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1700s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marlborough-duke-first.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="643" data-file-width="387" height="282" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Marlborough-duke-first.jpg/170px-Marlborough-duke-first.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Marlborough-duke-first.jpg/255px-Marlborough-duke-first.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Marlborough-duke-first.jpg/340px-Marlborough-duke-first.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marlborough-duke-first.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/John_Churchill,_1st_Duke_of_Marlborough" title="John Churchill, 1st Duke of Marlborough">John Churchill, 1st Duke of Marlborough</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="919" data-file-width="1450" height="108" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg/170px-Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg/255px-Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg/340px-Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marten%27s_Poltava.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Poltava" title="Battle of Poltava">Battle of Poltava</a> in 1709 turned the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">Russian Empire</a> into a European power.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1700" title="1700">1700</a>–<a href="/wiki/1721" title="1721">1721</a>: <a href="/wiki/Great_Northern_War" title="Great Northern War">Great Northern War</a> between <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tsarist_Russia" title="Tsarist Russia">Tsarist Russia</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Swedish_Empire" title="Swedish Empire">Swedish Empire</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1701" title="1701">1701</a>: <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Prussia" title="Kingdom of Prussia">Kingdom of Prussia</a> declared under King <a href="/wiki/Frederick_I_of_Prussia" title="Frederick I of Prussia">Frederick I</a>.</li>
<li>1701: <a href="/wiki/Ashanti_Empire" title="Ashanti Empire">Ashanti Empire</a> is formed under <a href="/wiki/Osei_Kofi_Tutu_I" title="Osei Kofi Tutu I">Osei Kofi Tutu I</a>.</li>
<li>1701–<a href="/wiki/1714" title="1714">1714</a>: The <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Spanish_Succession" title="War of the Spanish Succession">War of the Spanish Succession</a> is fought, involving most of continental <a href="/wiki/Louis_XIV_of_France#War_of_the_Spanish_Succession" title="Louis XIV of France">Europe</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>1701–<a href="/wiki/1702" title="1702">1702</a>: The <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Daily_Courant" title="Daily Courant">Daily Courant</a></i> and <i>The Norwich Post</i> become the first daily newspapers in England.</li>
<li>1702: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Forty-seven_Ronin" title="Forty-seven Ronin">Forty-seven Ronin</a> attack <a href="/wiki/Kira_Yoshinaka" title="Kira Yoshinaka">Kira Yoshinaka</a> and then commit <a href="/wiki/Seppuku" title="Seppuku">seppuku</a> in Japan.</li>
<li>1702–<a href="/wiki/1715" title="1715">1715</a>: <a href="/wiki/Camisard" title="Camisard">Camisard Rebellion</a> in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1703" title="1703">1703</a>: <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a> is founded by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peter_I_of_Russia" title="Peter I of Russia">Peter the Great</a>; it is the <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Capital_(political)" title="Capital (political)">capital</a> until <a href="/wiki/1918" title="1918">1918</a>.</li>
<li>1703–<a href="/wiki/1711" title="1711">1711</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/R%C3%A1k%C3%B3czi%27s_War_for_Independence" title="Rákóczi's War for Independence">Rákóczi Uprising</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Habsburg_Monarchy" title="Habsburg Monarchy">Habsburg Monarchy</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1704" title="1704">1704</a>: End of Japan's <a href="/wiki/Genroku" title="Genroku">Genroku</a> period.</li>
<li>1704: <a href="/wiki/First_Javanese_War_of_Succession" title="First Javanese War of Succession">First Javanese War of Succession</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp82_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp82-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1705" title="1705">1705</a>: <a href="/wiki/George_Frideric_Handel" title="George Frideric Handel">George Frideric Handel</a>'s first opera, <i><a href="/wiki/Almira" title="Almira">Almira</a></i>, premieres.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1706" title="1706">1706</a>: <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Spanish_Succession" title="War of the Spanish Succession">War of the Spanish Succession</a>: French troops defeated at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Ramillies" title="Battle of Ramillies">Battles of Ramilies</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Battle_of_Turin" title="Battle of Turin">and Turin</a>.</li>
<li>1706: The first English-language edition of the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arabian_Nights" title="Arabian Nights">Arabian Nights</a></i> is published.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1707" title="1707">1707</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Act_of_Union_1707" title="Act of Union 1707">Act of Union</a> is passed, merging the <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scottish</a> and <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> Parliaments, thus establishing the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Kingdom of Great Britain</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li>1707: After <a href="/wiki/Aurangzeb" title="Aurangzeb">Aurangzeb</a>'s death, the <a href="/wiki/Mughal_Empire" title="Mughal Empire">Mughal Empire</a> enters a long decline and the <a href="/wiki/Maratha_Empire" title="Maratha Empire">Maratha Empire</a> slowly replaces it.</li>
<li>1707: <a href="/wiki/Mount_Fuji" title="Mount Fuji">Mount Fuji</a> erupts in Japan for the first time since 1700.</li>
<li>1707: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_of_27_Years" title="War of 27 Years">War of 27 Years</a> between the Marathas and Mughals ends in India.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1708" title="1708">1708</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Honourable_East_India_Company" title="Honourable East India Company">The Company of Merchants of London Trading into the East Indies</a> and English Company Trading to the East Indies merge to form the United Company of Merchants of England Trading to the East Indies.</li>
<li>1708–<a href="/wiki/1709" title="1709">1709</a>: <a href="/wiki/Famine" title="Famine">Famine</a> kills one-third of <a href="/wiki/East_Prussia" title="East Prussia">East Prussia</a>'s population.</li>
<li>1709: The <a href="/wiki/Great_Frost_of_1709" title="Great Frost of 1709">Great Frost of 1709</a> marks the coldest winter in 500 years.</li>
<li>1709: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hotaki_dynasty" title="Hotaki dynasty">Hotaki dynasty</a> founded in Afghanistan.</li>
<li>1709: <a href="/wiki/Charles_XII_of_Sweden" title="Charles XII of Sweden">Charles XII of Sweden</a> flees to the Ottoman Empire after <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peter_I_of_Russia" title="Peter I of Russia">Peter I of Russia</a> defeats his army at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Poltava" title="Battle of Poltava">Battle of Poltava</a>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2550" data-file-width="2616" height="166" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg/170px-Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg/255px-Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg/340px-Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tokugawa_Yoshimune.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Tokugawa_Yoshimune" title="Tokugawa Yoshimune">Tokugawa Yoshimune</a>, Shogun of Japan</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1710s"><a href="/wiki/1710s" title="1710s">1710s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 1710s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1710" title="1710">1710</a>: The world's first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Copyright_law" title="Copyright law">copyright legislation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">Britain</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Anne" title="Statute of Anne">Statute of Anne</a>, takes effect.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1710" title="1710">1710</a>–<a href="/wiki/1711" title="1711">1711</a>: <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman Empire</a> fights Russia in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russo-Turkish_War_(1710%E2%80%931711)" title="Russo-Turkish War (1710–1711)">Russo-Turkish War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1711" title="1711">1711</a>–<a href="/wiki/1715" title="1715">1715</a>: <a href="/wiki/Tuscarora_War" title="Tuscarora War">Tuscarora War</a> between British, Dutch, and German settlers and the <a href="/wiki/Tuscarora_people" title="Tuscarora people">Tuscarora people</a> of <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1712" title="1712">1712</a>: <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Spanish_Succession" title="War of the Spanish Succession">War of the Spanish Succession</a>: The French defeat a combined Dutch-Austrian force at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Denain" title="Battle of Denain">Battle of Denain</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1712" title="1712">1712</a>: The first shipment of <a href="/wiki/Coffee" title="Coffee">coffee</a> from Java reaches <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MOORE90_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-MOORE90-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1713" title="1713">1713</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Utrecht" title="Treaty of Utrecht">Treaty of Utrecht</a> ends the <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Spanish_Succession" title="War of the Spanish Succession">War of the Spanish Succession</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1713" title="1713">1713</a>–<a href="/wiki/1714" title="1714">1714</a>: <a href="/wiki/Tarabai" title="Tarabai">Tarabai</a> establishes the rival <a href="/wiki/Maratha_Empire" title="Maratha Empire">Maratha Empire</a> government in <a href="/wiki/Kolhapur" title="Kolhapur">Kolhapur</a> against <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chattrapati_Shahu" title="Chattrapati Shahu">Chattrapati Shahu</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1714" title="1714">1714</a>: Accession of <a href="/wiki/George_I_of_Great_Britain" title="George I of Great Britain">George I</a>, Elector of Hanover, to the throne of Great Britain.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1715" title="1715">1715</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Jacobite_rising_of_1715" title="Jacobite rising of 1715">first Jacobite rising</a> breaks out; the British halt the Jacobite advance at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Sheriffmuir" title="Battle of Sheriffmuir">Battle of Sheriffmuir</a>; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Preston_(1715)" title="Battle of Preston (1715)">Battle of Preston</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1715" title="1715">1715</a>: <a href="/wiki/Louis_XIV_of_France" title="Louis XIV of France">Louis XIV</a> dies, leaving France greatly enlarged but deep in debt; <a href="/wiki/R%C3%A9gence" title="Régence">The Regency</a> takes power under <a href="/wiki/Philippe_II,_Duke_of_Orl%C3%A9ans" title="Philippe II, Duke of Orléans">Philippe d'Orleans</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1715" title="1715">1715</a>: <a href="/wiki/Pope_Clement_XI" title="Pope Clement XI">Pope Clement XI</a> <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Rites_controversy#Pope_Clement_XI.27s_decree" title="Chinese Rites controversy">declares</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Catholicism" title="Catholicism">Catholicism</a> and <a href="/wiki/Confucianism" title="Confucianism">Confucianism</a> incompatible.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1716" title="1716">1716</a>: Establishment of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sikh_Confederacy" title="Sikh Confederacy">Sikh Confederacy</a> along the present-day <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>-<a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> border.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1717" title="1717">1717</a>: The Netherlands, Britain and France sign the <a href="/wiki/Triple_Alliance_(1717)" title="Triple Alliance (1717)">Triple Alliance</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1717" title="1717">1717</a>: <a href="/wiki/Surabaya" title="Surabaya">Surabaya</a> rebels against the <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_India_Company" title="Dutch East India Company">VOC</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp84_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp84-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1718" title="1718">1718</a>: The city of <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">New Orleans</a> is founded by the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> in <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1718" title="1718">1718</a>: <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard" title="Blackbeard">Blackbeard</a> (Edward Teach) is killed by <a href="/wiki/Robert_Maynard" title="Robert Maynard">Robert Maynard</a> in a North Carolina inlet on the inner side of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ocracoke_Island" title="Ocracoke Island">Ocracoke Island</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1718" title="1718">1718</a>–<a href="/wiki/1730" title="1730">1730</a>: <a href="/wiki/Tulip_period" title="Tulip period">Tulip period</a> of the Ottoman Empire.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1719" title="1719">1719</a>: The Spanish attempt to restart the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jacobite_rising_of_1719" title="Jacobite rising of 1719">Jacobite rebellion</a> fails.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1719" title="1719">1719</a>: <a href="/wiki/Second_Javanese_War_of_Succession" title="Second Javanese War of Succession">Second Javanese War of Succession</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp84_10-1"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp84-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1720s"><a href="/wiki/1720s" title="1720s">1720s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 1720s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Europe,_1700_-_1714.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1086" data-file-width="1590" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Europe%2C_1700_-_1714.png/220px-Europe%2C_1700_-_1714.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Europe%2C_1700_-_1714.png/330px-Europe%2C_1700_-_1714.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Europe%2C_1700_-_1714.png/440px-Europe%2C_1700_-_1714.png 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Europe,_1700_-_1714.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Europe at the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Spanish_Succession" title="War of the Spanish Succession">War of the Spanish Succession</a>, 1700</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1720" title="1720">1720</a>: The <a href="/wiki/South_Sea_Company" title="South Sea Company">South Sea Bubble</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1720" title="1720">1720</a>: Spanish military embarks on the <a href="/wiki/Villasur_expedition" title="Villasur expedition">Villasur expedition</a>, traveling north from Mexico into the <a href="/wiki/Great_Plains" title="Great Plains">Great Plains</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1720" title="1720">1720</a>–<a href="/wiki/1721" title="1721">1721</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Great_Plague_of_Marseille" title="Great Plague of Marseille">Great Plague of Marseille</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1721" title="1721">1721</a>: <a href="/wiki/Robert_Walpole" title="Robert Walpole">Robert Walpole</a> becomes the first <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of Great Britain</a> (<a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">de facto</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1721" title="1721">1721</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Nystad" title="Treaty of Nystad">Treaty of Nystad</a> is signed, ending the <a href="/wiki/Great_Northern_War" title="Great Northern War">Great Northern War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1721" title="1721">1721</a>: <a href="/wiki/Kangxi_Emperor" title="Kangxi Emperor">Kangxi Emperor</a> <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Rites_controversy#Kangxi.27s_ban" title="Chinese Rites controversy">bans</a> Christian missionaries because of Pope Clement XI's decree.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1721" title="1721">1721</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Church_reform_of_Peter_I" title="Church reform of Peter I">Peter I reforms</a> the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Orthodox_Church" title="Russian Orthodox Church">Russian Orthodox Church</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1722" title="1722">1722</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pashtun_people" title="Pashtun people">Afghans</a> conquer Iran, overthrowing the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Safavids" title="Safavids">Safavid</a> <a href="/wiki/Sultan_Husayn" title="Sultan Husayn">Shah Sultan Husayn</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1722" title="1722">1722</a>: Kangxi Emperor of <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> dies.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1722" title="1722">1722</a>: <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Roberts" title="Bartholomew Roberts">Bartholomew Roberts</a> is killed in a sea battle off the African coast.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1722" title="1722">1722</a>–<a href="/wiki/1723" title="1723">1723</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russo-Persian_War,_1722-1723" title="Russo-Persian War, 1722-1723">Russo-Persian War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1722" title="1722">1722</a>–<a href="/wiki/1725" title="1725">1725</a>: Controversy over <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/William_Wood_(Mintmaster)" title="William Wood (Mintmaster)">William Wood</a>'s halfpence leads to the <i><a href="/wiki/Drapier%27s_Letters" title="Drapier's Letters">Drapier's Letters</a></i> and begins the Irish economic independence from England movement.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1723" title="1723">1723</a>: <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">Slavery</a> is abolished in Russia; <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peter_I_of_Russia" title="Peter I of Russia">Peter the Great</a> converts household <a href="/wiki/Slavery_in_medieval_Europe#Slavery_in_Russia" title="Slavery in medieval Europe">slaves</a> into house <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Serfs" title="Serfs">serfs</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1723" title="1723">1723</a>–<a href="/wiki/1730" title="1730">1730</a>: The "Great Disaster", an invasion of <a href="/wiki/Kazakhs" title="Kazakhs">Kazakh</a> territories by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dzungars" title="Dzungars">Dzungars</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1724" title="1724">1724</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Constantinople_(1724)" title="Treaty of Constantinople (1724)">Treaty of Constantinople</a> is signed, partitioning <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Persia" title="Persia">Persia</a> between the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman Empire</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1725" title="1725">1725</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Fula_people" title="Fula people">Fulani</a> nomads take complete control of <a href="/wiki/Imamate_of_Futa_Jallon" title="Imamate of Futa Jallon">Futa Jallon</a> and set up the first of many <a href="/wiki/Fula_jihads" title="Fula jihads">Fulani jihad states</a> to come.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1726" title="1726">1726</a>: The enormous Chinese encyclopedia <i><a href="/wiki/Gujin_Tushu_Jicheng" title="Gujin Tushu Jicheng">Gujin Tushu Jicheng</a></i> of over 100 million written <a href="/wiki/Chinese_characters" title="Chinese characters">Chinese characters</a> in over 800,000 pages is printed in 60 different copies using <a href="/wiki/Copper" title="Copper">copper</a>-based Chinese <a href="/wiki/Movable_type" title="Movable type">movable type</a> <a href="/wiki/Printing" title="Printing">printing</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1727" title="1727">1727</a>–<a href="/wiki/1729" title="1729">1729</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anglo-Spanish_War_(1727)" title="Anglo-Spanish War (1727)">Anglo-Spanish War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1729" title="1729">1729</a>–<a href="/wiki/1735" title="1735">1735</a>: <a href="/wiki/Charles_Wesley" title="Charles Wesley">Charles Wesley</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Wesley" title="John Wesley">John Wesley</a> begin <a href="/wiki/Methodism" title="Methodism">Methodism</a> in England.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1730s"><a href="/wiki/1730s" title="1730s">1730s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 1730s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="924" data-file-width="700" height="224" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg/170px-Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg/255px-Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg/340px-Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Portrait_of_the_Qianlong_Emperor_in_Court_Dress.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Qianlong_Emperor" title="Qianlong Emperor">Qianlong Emperor</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1730" title="1730">1730</a>: <a href="/wiki/Mahmud_I" title="Mahmud I">Mahmud I</a> takes over Ottoman Empire after the <a href="/wiki/Patrona_Halil" title="Patrona Halil">Patrona Halil</a> revolt, ending the <a href="/wiki/Tulip_period" title="Tulip period">Tulip period</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1730" title="1730">1730</a>–<a href="/wiki/1760" title="1760">1760</a>: The <a href="/wiki/First_Great_Awakening" title="First Great Awakening">First Great Awakening</a> takes place in Great Britain and North America.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1732" title="1732">1732</a>–<a href="/wiki/1734" title="1734">1734</a>: <a href="/wiki/Crimean_Khanate" title="Crimean Khanate">Crimean Tatar</a> raids into Russia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1733" title="1733">1733</a>–<a href="/wiki/1738" title="1738">1738</a>: <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Polish_Succession" title="War of the Polish Succession">War of the Polish Succession</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1734" title="1734">1734</a>: <a href="/wiki/Letters_on_the_English" title="Letters on the English">Letters Concerning on the English Nations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Voltaire" title="Voltaire">Voltaire</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1735" title="1735">1735</a>–<a href="/wiki/1739" title="1739">1739</a>: <a href="/wiki/Russo-Turkish_War_(1735%E2%80%931739)" title="Russo-Turkish War (1735–1739)">Russo-Turkish War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1735" title="1735">1735</a>–<a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Qianlong_Emperor" title="Qianlong Emperor">Qianlong Emperor</a> of China oversees a huge expansion in territory.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1735" title="1735">1735</a>: <a href="/wiki/Governor-General_of_the_Dutch_East_Indies" title="Governor-General of the Dutch East Indies">Governor-General</a> <a href="/wiki/Dirck_van_Cloon" title="Dirck van Cloon">Dirck van Cloon</a> dies, one of many victims of <a href="/wiki/Malaria" title="Malaria">malaria</a> in <a href="/wiki/Batavia,_Dutch_East_Indies" title="Batavia, Dutch East Indies">Batavia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp86_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp86-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1736" title="1736">1736</a>: <a href="/wiki/Nader_Shah" title="Nader Shah">Nader Shah</a> assumes the title of <a href="/wiki/Shah" title="Shah">Shah</a> of <a href="/wiki/History_of_Iran" title="History of Iran">Persia</a> and founds the <a href="/wiki/Afsharid_dynasty" title="Afsharid dynasty">Afsharid dynasty</a>; he rules until his death in <a href="/wiki/1747" title="1747">1747</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1736" title="1736">1736</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qing_Dynasty" title="Qing Dynasty">Qing Dynasty</a> Chinese court painters recreate <a href="/wiki/Zhang_Zeduan" title="Zhang Zeduan">Zhang Zeduan</a>'s classic <a href="/wiki/Panoramic_painting" title="Panoramic painting">panoramic painting</a>, <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Along_the_River_During_Qingming_Festival" title="Along the River During Qingming Festival">Along the River During Qingming Festival</a></i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1738" title="1738">1738</a>–<a href="/wiki/1756" title="1756">1756</a>: <a href="/wiki/List_of_famines" title="List of famines">Famine</a> across the <a href="/wiki/Sahel" title="Sahel">Sahel</a>; half the population of <a href="/wiki/Timbuktu" title="Timbuktu">Timbuktu</a> dies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1738" title="1738">1738</a>: <a href="/wiki/Pope_Clement_XII" title="Pope Clement XII">Pope Clement XII</a> issues <i><a href="/wiki/In_eminenti_apostolatus" title="In eminenti apostolatus">In eminenti apostolatus</a></i>, prohibiting Catholics from becoming <a href="/wiki/Freemasonry" title="Freemasonry">Freemasons</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1738" title="1738">1738</a>: <a href="/wiki/Turlough_O%27Carolan" title="Turlough O'Carolan">Turlough O'Carolan</a>, famous <a href="/wiki/Irish_people" title="Irish people">Irish</a> harper, dies.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1739" title="1739">1739</a>: <a href="/wiki/Nader_Shah" title="Nader Shah">Nader Shah</a> defeats the <a href="/wiki/Mughal_Empire" title="Mughal Empire">Mughals</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Karnal" title="Battle of Karnal">Battle of Karnal</a> and sacks <a href="/wiki/Delhi" title="Delhi">Delhi</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1739" title="1739">1739</a>: <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">Great Britain</a> and <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> fight the <a href="/wiki/War_of_Jenkins%27_Ear" title="War of Jenkins' Ear">War of Jenkins' Ear</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">Caribbean</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1740s"><a href="/wiki/1740s" title="1740s">1740s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 1740s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1110" data-file-width="796" height="237" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png/170px-Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png/255px-Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png/340px-Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Frederick_II_of_Prussia_Coloured_drawing.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Frederick_II_of_Prussia" title="Frederick II of Prussia">Frederick II the Great</a>, King of Prussia</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="892" data-file-width="1498" height="101" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg/170px-The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg/255px-The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg/340px-The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:The_Battle_of_Culloden.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The extinction of the <a href="/wiki/Scottish_clan" title="Scottish clan">Scottish clan</a> system came with the defeat of the clansmen at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Culloden" title="Battle of Culloden">Battle of Culloden</a> in 1746<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1740" title="1740">1740</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Frederick_II_of_Prussia" title="Frederick II of Prussia">Frederick the Great</a> comes to power in <a href="/wiki/Prussia" title="Prussia">Prussia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1740" title="1740">1740</a>: <a href="/wiki/Great_Awakening" title="Great Awakening">Great Awakening</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_Whitefield" title="George Whitefield">George Whitefield</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1740" title="1740">1740</a>: The British attempt to capture <a href="/wiki/St._Augustine,_Florida" title="St. Augustine, Florida">St. Augustine, Florida</a> but lose to the Spanish during the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Siege_of_St._Augustine" title="Siege of St. Augustine">Siege of St. Augustine</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1740" title="1740">1740</a>–<a href="/wiki/1741" title="1741">1741</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Great_Irish_Famine_(1740%E2%80%931741)" title="Great Irish Famine (1740–1741)">Famine in Ireland</a> kills ten percent of the population.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1740" title="1740">1740</a>–<a href="/wiki/1748" title="1748">1748</a>: <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Austrian_Succession" title="War of the Austrian Succession">War of the Austrian Succession</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1740" title="1740">1740</a>: 9 October, a massacre of Batavia's ethnic Chinese begins after they are suspected by the VOC of planning a rebellion; approximately 10,000 are killed and the Chinese quarter is burned.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp87_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp87-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1741" title="1741">1741</a>: <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russians</a> begin settling the <a href="/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1741" title="1741">1741</a>: <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XIV" title="Pope Benedict XIV">Pope Benedict XIV</a> issues <i>Immensa Pastorum principis</i> against slavery.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1742" title="1742">1742</a>: The rebellion of <a href="/wiki/Juan_Santos_Atahualpa" title="Juan Santos Atahualpa">Juan Santos Atahualpa</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1742" title="1742">1742</a>: <a href="/wiki/Marvel%27s_Mill" title="Marvel's Mill">Marvel's Mill</a>, the first water-powered <a href="/wiki/Cotton_mill" title="Cotton mill">cotton mill</a>, begins operation in England.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1743" title="1743">1743</a>: The capital of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sultanate_of_Mataram" title="Sultanate of Mataram">Sultanate of Mataram</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kartasura" title="Kartasura">Kartasura</a> fell under Geger Pecinan uprising — Raden Mas Garendi (Sunan Kuning) led Chinese mercenaries revolted against Pakubuwono II.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1744" title="1744">1744</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/First_Saudi_State" title="First Saudi State">First Saudi State</a> is founded by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mohammed_Ibn_Saud" title="Mohammed Ibn Saud">Mohammed Ibn Saud</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1744" title="1744">1744</a>: The French attempt to restart the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jacobite_Rising#1744_French_invasion_attempt" title="Jacobite Rising">Jacobite rebellion</a> fails.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1744" title="1744">1744</a>–<a href="/wiki/1748" title="1748">1748</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Carnatic_Wars" title="Carnatic Wars">First Carnatic War</a> is fought between the <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a>, the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marathas" title="Marathas">Marathas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mysore" title="Mysore">Mysore</a> in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1745" title="1745">1745</a>: <a href="/wiki/Jacobite_rising_of_1745" title="Jacobite rising of 1745">Second Jacobite rising</a> is begun by <a href="/wiki/Charles_Edward_Stuart" title="Charles Edward Stuart">Charles Edward Stuart</a> in <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1745" title="1745">1745</a>: 17 February, <a href="/wiki/Pakubuwono_II" title="Pakubuwono II">Pakubuwono II</a> establishes a new <a href="/wiki/Kraton_(Indonesia)" title="Kraton (Indonesia)">kraton</a> in Sala village, along with <a href="/wiki/Surakarta_Sunanate" title="Surakarta Sunanate">Surakarta Sunanate</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1747" title="1747">1747</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ahmed_Shah_Durrani" title="Ahmed Shah Durrani">Ahmed Shah Durrani</a> founds the <a href="/wiki/Durrani_Empire" title="Durrani Empire">Durrani Empire</a> in modern-day <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1748" title="1748">1748</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Aix-la-Chapelle_(1748)" title="Treaty of Aix-la-Chapelle (1748)">Treaty of Aix-La-Chapelle</a> ends the War of the Austrian Succession and First Carnatic War.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1748" title="1748">1748</a>–<a href="/wiki/1754" title="1754">1754</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Carnatic_Wars" title="Carnatic Wars">Second Carnatic War</a> is fought between the British, the French, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marathas" title="Marathas">Marathas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mysore" title="Mysore">Mysore</a> in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1750s"><a href="/wiki/1750s" title="1750s">1750s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 1750s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Benjamin_West_005.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3456" height="113" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Benjamin_West_005.jpg/170px-Benjamin_West_005.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Benjamin_West_005.jpg/255px-Benjamin_West_005.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Benjamin_West_005.jpg/340px-Benjamin_West_005.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Benjamin_West_005.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/The_Death_of_General_Wolfe" title="The Death of General Wolfe">The Death of General Wolfe</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1750" title="1750">1750</a>: Peak of the <a href="/wiki/Little_Ice_Age" title="Little Ice Age">Little Ice Age</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1754" title="1754">1754</a>: The Treaty of Pondicherry ends the Second Carnatic War and recognizes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Muhammed_Ali_Khan_Wallajah" title="Muhammed Ali Khan Wallajah">Muhammed Ali Khan Wallajah</a> as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nawab_of_the_Carnatic" title="Nawab of the Carnatic">Nawab of the Carnatic</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1754" title="1754">1754</a>: <a href="/wiki/Columbia_University" title="Columbia University">King's College</a> is founded by a royal charter of <a href="/wiki/George_II_of_Great_Britain" title="George II of Great Britain">George II of Great Britain</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1754" title="1754">1754</a>–<a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: The <a href="/wiki/French_and_Indian_War" title="French and Indian War">French and Indian War</a>, the North American chapter of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Years%27_War" title="Seven Years' War">Seven Years' War</a>, is fought in colonial North America, mostly by the French and their allies against the English and their allies.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1755" title="1755">1755</a>: The <a href="/wiki/1755_Lisbon_earthquake" title="1755 Lisbon earthquake">Lisbon earthquake</a> occurs.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1755" title="1755">1755</a>–<a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Great_Upheaval" title="Great Upheaval">Great Upheaval</a> forces transfer of the French Acadian population from Nova Scotia and New Brunswick.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1755" title="1755">1755</a>: 13 February, the Treaty of Giyanti is signed, effectively partitioning the <a href="/wiki/Mataram_Sultanate" title="Mataram Sultanate">Mataram Sultanate</a>; the VOC recognizes Mangkubumi as Sultan Hamengkubuwana I, who rules half of Central Java; Hamengkubuwana I then establishes <a href="/wiki/Yogyakarta_Sultanate" title="Yogyakarta Sultanate">Yogyakarta Sultanate</a>, moves to Yogya and renames the city <a href="/wiki/Yogyakarta" title="Yogyakarta">Yogyakarta</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp93_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp93-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1755" title="1755">1755</a>: Demand-Supply, <a href="/wiki/Richard_Cantillon" title="Richard Cantillon">Richard Cantillon</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1756" title="1756">1756</a>–<a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Seven_Years%27_War" title="Seven Years' War">Seven Years' War</a> is fought among European powers in various theaters around the world.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1756" title="1756">1756</a>–<a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Carnatic_Wars" title="Carnatic Wars">Third Carnatic War</a> is fought between the <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a>, the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marathas" title="Marathas">Marathas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mysore" title="Mysore">Mysore</a> in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1757" title="1757">1757</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Plassey" title="Battle of Plassey">Battle of Plassey</a> signals the beginning of formal <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">British</a> rule in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> after years of commercial activity under the auspices of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Honourable_East_India_Company" title="Honourable East India Company">East India Company</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1757" title="1757">1757</a>: 17 March, Salatiga treaty between <a href="/wiki/Mangkunegara_I" title="Mangkunegara I">Prince Sambernyawa</a> with <a href="/wiki/Pakubuwono_III" title="Pakubuwono III">Pakubuwono III</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hamengkubuwono_I" title="Hamengkubuwono I">Hamengkubuwono I</a> further partitions the remnant of Mataram Sultanate; the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mangkunegaran" title="Mangkunegaran">Mangkunegaran</a> Grand Duchy is established.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1758" title="1758">1758</a>: British colonel <a href="/wiki/James_Wolfe" title="James Wolfe">James Wolfe</a> issues <a href="/wiki/Wolfe%27s_Manifesto" title="Wolfe's Manifesto">Wolfe's Manifesto</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1759" title="1759">1759</a>: <a href="/wiki/French_and_Indian_War" title="French and Indian War">French and Indian War</a>: French commander <a href="/wiki/Louis-Joseph_de_Montcalm" title="Louis-Joseph de Montcalm">Louis-Joseph de Montcalm</a> and British commander <a href="/wiki/James_Wolfe" title="James Wolfe">James Wolfe</a> die during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Plains_of_Abraham" title="Battle of the Plains of Abraham">Battle of the Plains of Abraham</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1760s"><a href="/wiki/1760s" title="1760s">1760s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 1760s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1255" data-file-width="866" height="246" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/50/Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg/170px-Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/50/Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg/255px-Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/50/Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg/340px-Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Catherinethegreatroslin.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Catherine_the_Great" title="Catherine the Great">Catherine the Great</a>, Empress of Russia.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3801" data-file-width="2433" height="266" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg/170px-Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg/255px-Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg/340px-Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Allan_Ramsay_-_King_George_III_in_coronation_robes_-_Google_Art_Project.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/George_III_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="George III of the United Kingdom">George III</a>, King of Great Britain.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1760" title="1760">1760</a>: <a href="/wiki/George_III_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="George III of the United Kingdom">George III</a> becomes King of Britain.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1760" title="1760">1760</a>: <a href="/wiki/Zand_dynasty" title="Zand dynasty">Zand dynasty</a> is founded in Iran.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1761" title="1761">1761</a>: Maratha Empire defeated at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Battle_of_Panipat_(1761)" title="Battle of Panipat (1761)">Battle of Panipat</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1762" title="1762">1762</a>–<a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>: Reign of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Catherine_II_of_Russia" title="Catherine II of Russia">Catherine the Great</a> of <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Paris_(1763)" title="Treaty of Paris (1763)">Treaty of Paris</a> ends the Seven Years' War and Third Carnatic War.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Mysore" title="Kingdom of Mysore">Kingdom of Mysore</a> conquers the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Keladi_Nayaka" title="Keladi Nayaka">Kingdom of Keladi</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: <a href="/wiki/Echelon_formation" title="Echelon formation">Echelon Formation</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Frederick_II_of_Prussia" title="Frederick II of Prussia">Frederick II of Prussia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1765" title="1765">1765</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Stamp_Act_1765" title="Stamp Act 1765">Stamp Act</a> is introduced into the <a href="/wiki/Thirteen_Colonies" title="Thirteen Colonies">American colonies</a> by the British Parliament.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1766" title="1766">1766</a>: <a href="/wiki/Christian_VII_of_Denmark" title="Christian VII of Denmark">Christian VII</a> becomes king of <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a>. He was <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Denmark" title="Kingdom of Denmark">king of Denmark</a> to <a href="/wiki/1808" title="1808">1808</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1766" title="1766">1766</a>–<a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: <a href="/wiki/Anglo-Mysore_Wars" title="Anglo-Mysore Wars">Anglo-Mysore Wars</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1767" title="1767">1767</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Konbaung_Dynasty" title="Konbaung Dynasty">Burmese</a> conquer the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ayutthaya_kingdom" title="Ayutthaya kingdom">Ayutthaya kingdom</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1768" title="1768">1768</a>: <a href="/wiki/Gurkha" title="Gurkha">Gurkhas</a> conquer <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepal</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1768" title="1768">1768</a>–<a href="/wiki/1772" title="1772">1772</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_of_the_Bar_Confederation" title="War of the Bar Confederation">War of the Bar Confederation</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1768" title="1768">1768</a>–<a href="/wiki/1774" title="1774">1774</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russo-Turkish_War,_1768-1774" title="Russo-Turkish War, 1768-1774">Russo-Turkish War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1768" title="1768">1768</a>: <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Leather" title="Imperial Leather">Imperial Leather</a>, <a href="/wiki/Orlov_(family)" title="Orlov (family)">Count Olov</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1769" title="1769">1769</a>: <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spanish</a> <a href="/wiki/Missionary" title="Missionary">missionaries</a> establish the first of 21 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spanish_Missions_of_California" title="Spanish Missions of California">missions</a> in <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1769" title="1769">1769</a>–<a href="/wiki/1770" title="1770">1770</a>: <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a> explores and maps New Zealand and Australia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1769" title="1769">1769</a>–<a href="/wiki/1773" title="1773">1773</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bengal_famine_of_1770" title="Bengal famine of 1770">Bengal famine of 1770</a> kills one-third of the <a href="/wiki/Bengal" title="Bengal">Bengal</a> population.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1769" title="1769">1769</a>: French expeditions capture <a href="/wiki/Clove" title="Clove">clove</a> plants in <a href="/wiki/Ambon_Island" title="Ambon Island">Ambon</a>, ending the VOC monopoly of the plant.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp102_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp102-22">[22]</a></sup> (to 1772)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1769" title="1769">1769</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Court_Factor" title="Court Factor">Court Factor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mayer_Amschel_Rothschild" title="Mayer Amschel Rothschild">Mayer Amschel Rothschild</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1770s"><a href="/wiki/1770s" title="1770s">1770s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 1770s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="5120" data-file-width="3133" height="278" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg/170px-Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg/255px-Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg/340px-Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Encyclopedie_de_D%27Alembert_et_Diderot_-_Premiere_Page_-_ENC_1-NA5.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Encyclop%C3%A9die,_ou_dictionnaire_raisonn%C3%A9_des_sciences,_des_arts_et_des_m%C3%A9tiers" title="Encyclopédie, ou dictionnaire raisonné des sciences, des arts et des métiers">Encyclopédie, ou dictionnaire raisonné des sciences, des arts et des métiers</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1447" data-file-width="2546" height="97" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg/170px-Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg/255px-Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg/340px-Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Rejtan_Upadek_Polski_Matejko.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Tadeusz_Rejtan" title="Tadeusz Rejtan">Rejtan</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Partitions_of_Poland" title="Partitions of Poland">Partitions of Poland</a> on <a href="/wiki/Rejtan_(painting)" title="Rejtan (painting)">a painting</a> by <a href="/wiki/Jan_Matejko" title="Jan Matejko">Jan Matejko</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1770" title="1770">1770</a>: <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a> claims the East Coast of Australia (<a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales" title="New South Wales">New South Wales</a>) for Great Britain.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1770" title="1770">1770</a>: 5 March, the <a href="/wiki/Boston_Massacre" title="Boston Massacre">Boston Massacre</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1770" title="1770">1770</a>–<a href="/wiki/1771" title="1771">1771</a>: <a href="/wiki/Famines_in_Czech_lands" title="Famines in Czech lands">Famine in Czech lands</a> kills hundreds of thousands.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1770" title="1770">1770</a>: <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a> stops at Onrust Island in the Bay of Batavia for repairs to his ship <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HM_Bark_Endeavour" title="HM Bark Endeavour">Endeavour</a></i> on his voyage around the world.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HEUKEN307_23-0"><a href="#cite_note-HEUKEN307-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1771" title="1771">1771</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Plague_Riot" title="Plague Riot">Plague Riot</a> in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1771" title="1771">1771</a>: <a href="/wiki/Richard_Arkwright" title="Richard Arkwright">Richard Arkwright</a> and his partners build the world's first water-powered mill at Cromford.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1772" title="1772">1772</a>: Reformer <a href="/wiki/Johann_Friedrich_Struensee" title="Johann Friedrich Struensee">Johann Friedrich Struensee</a> executed in <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1772" title="1772">1772</a>: <a href="/wiki/Gustav_III_of_Sweden" title="Gustav III of Sweden">Gustav III of Sweden</a> stages a coup d'état, becoming almost an absolute monarch.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1772" title="1772">1772</a>–<a href="/wiki/1779" title="1779">1779</a>: Maratha Empire fights Britain and <a href="/wiki/Raghunathrao" title="Raghunathrao">Raghunathrao</a>'s forces during the <a href="/wiki/First_Anglo-Maratha_War" title="First Anglo-Maratha War">First Anglo-Maratha War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1772" title="1772">1772</a>–<a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Partitions_of_Poland" title="Partitions of Poland">Partitions of Poland</a> end the <a href="/wiki/Polish%E2%80%93Lithuanian_Commonwealth" title="Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth">Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth</a> and erase Poland from the map for 123 years.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1773" title="1773">1773</a>–<a href="/wiki/1775" title="1775">1775</a>: <a href="/wiki/Pugachev%27s_Rebellion" title="Pugachev's Rebellion">Pugachev's Rebellion</a>, the largest peasant revolt in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> history.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1773" title="1773">1773</a>: East India Company starts operations in <a href="/wiki/Bengal" title="Bengal">Bengal</a> to smuggle <a href="/wiki/First_Opium_War" title="First Opium War">opium into China</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1773" title="1773">1773</a>: 16 December, the <a href="/wiki/Boston_Tea_Party" title="Boston Tea Party">Boston Tea Party</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1775" title="1775">1775</a>: <a href="/wiki/John_Harrison" title="John Harrison">John Harrison H4</a> and <a href="/wiki/Larcum_Kendall" title="Larcum Kendall">Larcum Kendall K1</a> <a href="/wiki/Marine_chronometer" title="Marine chronometer">marine chronometers</a> are used to measure <a href="/wiki/Longitude" title="Longitude">longitude</a> by <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a> on his <a href="/wiki/James_Cook#Second_voyage_.281772.E2.80.9375.29" title="James Cook">second voyage (1772–1775)</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1775" title="1775">1775</a>–<a href="/wiki/1782" title="1782">1782</a>: <a href="/wiki/First_Anglo-Maratha_War" title="First Anglo-Maratha War">First Anglo-Maratha War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1775" title="1775">1775</a>–<a href="/wiki/1783" title="1783">1783</a>: <a href="/wiki/American_Revolutionary_War" title="American Revolutionary War">American Revolutionary War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>: <a href="/wiki/Illuminati" title="Illuminati">Illuminati</a> founded by <a href="/wiki/Adam_Weishaupt" title="Adam Weishaupt">Adam Weishaupt</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>: The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Declaration_of_Independence" title="United States Declaration of Independence">United States Declaration of Independence</a> is adopted by the <a href="/wiki/Continental_Congress" title="Continental Congress">Continental Congress</a> in <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>: <a href="/wiki/Adam_Smith" title="Adam Smith">Adam Smith</a> publishes <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wealth_of_Nations" title="The Wealth of Nations">The Wealth of Nations</a></i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1778" title="1778">1778</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/T%C3%A2y_S%C6%A1n_Dynasty" title="Tây Sơn Dynasty">Tây Sơn Dynasty</a> is established in <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1778" title="1778">1778</a>: <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a> becomes the first European to land on the <a href="/wiki/Hawaiian_Islands" title="Hawaiian Islands">Hawaiian Islands</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1778" title="1778">1778</a>: 24 April, the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Batavian_Society_of_Arts_and_Sciences" title="Royal Batavian Society of Arts and Sciences">Royal Batavian Society of Arts and Sciences</a> is established by a group of Dutch intellectuals;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> this institution is a pioneer of scientific efforts in Indonesia and the founder of the <a href="/wiki/National_Museum_of_Indonesia" title="National Museum of Indonesia">National Museum of Indonesia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1779" title="1779">1779</a>: Captain <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a> is killed by <a href="/wiki/Native_Hawaiians" title="Native Hawaiians">Hawaiian natives</a> at <a href="/wiki/Kealakekua_Bay" title="Kealakekua Bay">Kealakekua Bay</a>, following an attempted kidnapping and ransoming of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ruling_chiefs_of_Hawaii" title="Ruling chiefs of Hawaii">ruling chief</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kalani%CA%BB%C5%8Dpu%CA%BBu" title="Kalaniʻōpuʻu">Kalaniʻōpuʻu</a> in return for a stolen boat.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1779" title="1779">1779</a>–<a href="/wiki/1879" title="1879">1879</a>: <a href="/wiki/Xhosa_Wars" title="Xhosa Wars">Xhosa Wars</a> between British and <a href="/wiki/Boer" title="Boer">Boer</a> settlers and the <a href="/wiki/Xhosa_people" title="Xhosa people">Xhosas</a> in the <a href="/wiki/South_African_Republic" title="South African Republic">South African Republic</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1780s"><a href="/wiki/1780s" title="1780s">1780s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 1780s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1159" data-file-width="963" height="205" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png/170px-Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png/255px-Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png/340px-Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Portrait_of_George_Washington-transparent.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/George_Washington" title="George Washington">George Washington</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1533" data-file-width="1165" height="224" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg/170px-Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg/255px-Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg/340px-Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen_in_1789.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen" title="Declaration of the Rights of Man and of the Citizen">Declaration of the Rights of Man and of the Citizen</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1780" title="1780">1780</a>: Outbreak of the <a href="/wiki/Rebellion_of_T%C3%BApac_Amaru_II" title="Rebellion of Túpac Amaru II">indigenous rebellion</a> against Spanish colonization led by <a href="/wiki/T%C3%BApac_Amaru_II" title="Túpac Amaru II">Túpac Amaru II</a> in <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1781" title="1781">1781</a>: The city of <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a> is founded by <a href="/wiki/Spaniards" title="Spaniards">Spanish</a> settlers.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1781" title="1781">1781</a>–<a href="/wiki/1785" title="1785">1785</a>: <a href="/wiki/Serfdom" title="Serfdom">Serfdom</a> is abolished in the <a href="/wiki/Habsburg_Monarchy" title="Habsburg Monarchy">Austrian monarchy</a> (first step; second step in <a href="/wiki/1848" title="1848">1848</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1783" title="1783">1783</a>: <a href="/wiki/List_of_famines" title="List of famines">Famine</a> in <a href="/wiki/Iceland" title="Iceland">Iceland</a>, caused by the eruption of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Laki_(volcano)" title="Laki (volcano)">Laki</a> volcano.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1783" title="1783">1783</a>: <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">Russian Empire</a> annexes the <a href="/wiki/Crimean_Khanate" title="Crimean Khanate">Crimean Khanate</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1783" title="1783">1783</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Paris_(1783)" title="Treaty of Paris (1783)">Treaty of Paris</a> formally ends the <a href="/wiki/American_Revolutionary_War" title="American Revolutionary War">American Revolutionary War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1785" title="1785">1785</a>–<a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>: Imam <a href="/wiki/Sheikh_Mansur" title="Sheikh Mansur">Sheikh Mansur</a>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chechen_people" title="Chechen people">Chechen</a> warrior and Muslim mystic, leads a coalition of Muslim <a href="/wiki/Peoples_of_the_Caucasus" title="Peoples of the Caucasus">Caucasian tribes</a> from throughout the <a href="/wiki/Caucasus" title="Caucasus">Caucasus</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Jihad" title="Jihad">holy war</a> against Russian settlers and military bases in the Caucasus, as well as against local traditionalists, who followed the traditional customs and common law (Adat) rather than the theocratic Sharia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1785" title="1785">1785</a>–<a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Northwest_Indian_War" title="Northwest Indian War">Northwest Indian War</a> is fought between the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indigenous_peoples_in_the_United_States" title="Indigenous peoples in the United States">Native Americans</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1787" title="1787">1787</a>: The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Constitution" title="United States Constitution">United States Constitution</a> is written in <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</a> and submitted to the states for ratification.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1787" title="1787">1787</a>: Freed slaves from <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> establish <a href="/wiki/Freetown" title="Freetown">Freetown</a> in present-day <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1787" title="1787">1787</a>: <a href="/wiki/Kansei_Reforms" title="Kansei Reforms">Kansei Reforms</a> instituted in Japan by <a href="/wiki/Matsudaira_Sadanobu" title="Matsudaira Sadanobu">Matsudaira Sadanobu</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1787" title="1787">1787</a>–<a href="/wiki/1792" title="1792">1792</a>: <a href="/wiki/Russo-Turkish_War_(1787%E2%80%931792)" title="Russo-Turkish War (1787–1792)">Russo-Turkish War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>: First French <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quaker" title="Quaker">Quaker</a> community established in <a href="/wiki/Cong%C3%A9nies" title="Congénies">Congénies</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>: First permanent European settlement established in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> by Britain at <a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>–<a href="/wiki/1790" title="1790">1790</a>: <a href="/wiki/Russo-Swedish_War_(1788%E2%80%931790)" title="Russo-Swedish War (1788–1790)">Russo-Swedish War (1788–1790)</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>: <a href="/wiki/New_Hampshire" title="New Hampshire">New Hampshire</a> becomes the 9th state to ratify the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Constitution" title="United States Constitution">United States Constitution</a>, and by the terms of Article VII it takes effect.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>–<a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: <a href="/wiki/Colonial_Brazil#Inconfid.C3.AAncia_Mineira" title="Colonial Brazil">Inconfidência Mineira</a>, conspiracy against the colonial authorities in <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: <a href="/wiki/George_Washington" title="George Washington">George Washington</a> is elected the first <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a>; he serves until <a href="/wiki/1797" title="1797">1797</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: <a href="/wiki/Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_Man_and_of_the_Citizen" title="Declaration of the Rights of Man and of the Citizen">Declaration of the Rights of Man and of the Citizen</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: Great Britain and Spain dispute the <a href="/wiki/Nootka_Sound" title="Nootka Sound">Nootka Sound</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Nootka_Crisis" title="Nootka Crisis">Nootka Crisis</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>–<a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: <a href="/wiki/French_Revolution" title="French Revolution">French Revolution</a>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1801_Antoine-Jean_Gros_-_Bonaparte_on_the_Bridge_at_Arcole.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1400" data-file-width="990" height="240" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/1801_Antoine-Jean_Gros_-_Bonaparte_on_the_Bridge_at_Arcole.jpg/170px-1801_Antoine-Jean_Gros_-_Bonaparte_on_the_Bridge_at_Arcole.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/1801_Antoine-Jean_Gros_-_Bonaparte_on_the_Bridge_at_Arcole.jpg/255px-1801_Antoine-Jean_Gros_-_Bonaparte_on_the_Bridge_at_Arcole.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/1801_Antoine-Jean_Gros_-_Bonaparte_on_the_Bridge_at_Arcole.jpg/340px-1801_Antoine-Jean_Gros_-_Bonaparte_on_the_Bridge_at_Arcole.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
