</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Li%C3%A8ge_Revolution" title="Liège Revolution">Liège Revolution</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Brabant_Revolution" title="Brabant Revolution">Brabant Revolution</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1790s"><a href="/wiki/1790s" title="1790s">1790s</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 1790s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1790" title="1790">1790</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_of_Belgium" title="United States of Belgium">United States of Belgium</a> is proclaimed following the <a href="/wiki/Brabant_Revolution" title="Brabant Revolution">Brabant Revolution</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1790" title="1790">1790</a>: Suppression of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_of_Belgium" title="United States of Belgium">United States of Belgium</a> and re-establishment of <a href="/wiki/Austrian_Netherlands" title="Austrian Netherlands">Austrian control</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1790" title="1790">1790</a>: Establishment of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish-Prussian_Pact" title="Polish-Prussian Pact">Polish-Prussian Pact</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>: The Constitutional Act (or Canada Act) creates the two provinces of <a href="/wiki/Upper_Canada" title="Upper Canada">Upper</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lower_Canada" title="Lower Canada">Lower Canada</a> in <a href="/wiki/British_North_America" title="British North America">British North America</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>: Suppression of the <a href="/wiki/Li%C3%A8ge_Revolution" title="Liège Revolution">Liège Revolution</a> by <a href="/wiki/Holy_Roman_Empire" title="Holy Roman Empire">Austrian</a> forces and re-establishment of the <a href="/wiki/Prince-Bishopric_of_Li%C3%A8ge" title="Prince-Bishopric of Liège">Prince-Bishopric of Liège</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>–<a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: <a href="/wiki/George_Vancouver" title="George Vancouver">George Vancouver</a> explores the world during the <a href="/wiki/Vancouver_Expedition" title="Vancouver Expedition">Vancouver Expedition</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>–<a href="/wiki/1804" title="1804">1804</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Haitian_Revolution" title="Haitian Revolution">Haitian Revolution</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>: Surprise Symphony, <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Haydn" title="Joseph Haydn">Hyden</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1792" title="1792">1792</a>–<a href="/wiki/1802" title="1802">1802</a>: The <a href="/wiki/French_Revolutionary_Wars" title="French Revolutionary Wars">French Revolutionary Wars</a> lead into the <a href="/wiki/Napoleonic_Wars" title="Napoleonic Wars">Napoleonic Wars</a>, which last from <a href="/wiki/1803" title="1803">1803</a>–<a href="/wiki/1815" title="1815">1815</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1792" title="1792">1792</a>: The <a href="/wiki/New_York_Stock_Exchange" title="New York Stock Exchange">New York Stock &amp; Exchange Board</a> is founded.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1792" title="1792">1792</a>: <a href="/wiki/Polish%E2%80%93Russian_War_of_1792" title="Polish–Russian War of 1792">Polish–Russian War of 1792</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1792" title="1792">1792</a>: King <a href="/wiki/Gustav_III_of_Sweden" title="Gustav III of Sweden">Gustav III of Sweden</a> is assassinated by a conspiracy of noblemen.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1792" title="1792">1792</a>: March, Hamengkubuwana I dies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp101_26-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp101-26">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1793" title="1793">1793</a>: Former King <a href="/wiki/Louis_XVI_of_France" title="Louis XVI of France">Louis XVI of France</a> and his wife <a href="/wiki/Marie_Antoinette" title="Marie Antoinette">Marie Antoinette</a> are <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guillotined" title="Guillotined">guillotined</a>. Louis is executed in January, Marie Antoinette in October.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1793" title="1793">1793</a>: <a href="/wiki/Upper_Canada" title="Upper Canada">Upper Canada</a> <a href="/wiki/Act_Against_Slavery" title="Act Against Slavery">bans slavery</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1793" title="1793">1793</a>: The largest <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yellow_Fever_Epidemic_of_1793" title="Yellow Fever Epidemic of 1793">yellow fever epidemic</a> in American history kills as many as 5,000 people in <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</a>, roughly 10% of the population.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1793" title="1793">1793</a>–<a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Revolt_in_the_Vend%C3%A9e" title="Revolt in the Vendée">Revolt in the Vendée</a> against the French Republic at the time of the <a href="/wiki/French_Revolution" title="French Revolution">Revolution</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1794" title="1794">1794</a>: <a href="/wiki/Ko%C5%9Bciuszko_Uprising" title="Kościuszko Uprising">Polish revolt</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1794" title="1794">1794</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jay%27s_Treaty" title="Jay's Treaty">Jay's Treaty</a> is concluded between <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">Great Britain</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, by which the Western outposts in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Lakes" title="Great Lakes">Great Lakes</a> are returned to the U.S. and commerce between the two countries is regulated.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1794" title="1794">1794</a>: <a href="/wiki/Qajar_dynasty" title="Qajar dynasty">Qajar dynasty</a> founded in Iran after replacing the Zand dynasty.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1794" title="1794">1794</a>: <a href="/wiki/The_Mysteries_of_Udolpho" title="The Mysteries of Udolpho">The Mysteries of Udolpho</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ann_Radcliffe" title="Ann Radcliffe">Ann Radcliffe</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mohammad_Khan_Qajar" title="Mohammad Khan Qajar">Mohammad Khan Qajar</a> razes <a href="/wiki/Tbilisi" title="Tbilisi">Tbilisi</a> to the ground.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: Establishment of the French-backed <a href="/wiki/Batavian_Republic" title="Batavian Republic">Batavian Republic</a> in present-day <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: <a href="/wiki/Pinckney%27s_Treaty" title="Pinckney's Treaty">Pinckney's Treaty</a> between the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> grants the <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_Territory" title="Mississippi Territory">Mississippi Territory</a> to the U.S.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marseillaise" title="Marseillaise">Marseillaise</a> is officially adopted as the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a> <a href="/wiki/National_anthem" title="National anthem">national anthem</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: <a href="/wiki/Kamehameha_I" title="Kamehameha I">Kamehameha I</a> of the Island of <a href="/wiki/Hawaii_(island)" title="Hawaii (island)">Hawaii</a> defeats the <a href="/wiki/Oahu" title="Oahu">Oahuans</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Battle_of_Nu%27uanu" title="Battle of Nu'uanu">Battle of Nu'uanu</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>: <a href="/wiki/Edward_Jenner" title="Edward Jenner">Edward Jenner</a> administers the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Smallpox_vaccination" title="Smallpox vaccination">smallpox vaccination</a>; <a href="/wiki/Smallpox" title="Smallpox">smallpox</a> killed an estimated 400,000 Europeans each year during the 18th century, including five reigning <a href="/wiki/Monarch" title="Monarch">monarchs</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>: <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_First_Coalition" title="War of the First Coalition">War of the First Coalition</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Montenotte" title="Battle of Montenotte">Battle of Montenotte</a> marks <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Napoleon_Bonaparte" title="Napoleon Bonaparte">Napoleon Bonaparte</a>'s first victory as an army commander.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>: The British eject the Dutch from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ceylon" title="Ceylon">Ceylon</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>: <a href="/wiki/Mungo_Park_(explorer)" title="Mungo Park (explorer)">Mungo Park</a>, backed by the <a href="/wiki/African_Association" title="African Association">African Association</a>, is the first European to set eyes on the <a href="/wiki/Niger_River" title="Niger River">Niger River</a> in Africa.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>–<a href="/wiki/1804" title="1804">1804</a>: The <a href="/wiki/White_Lotus_Rebellion" title="White Lotus Rebellion">White Lotus Rebellion</a> against the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qing_Dynasty" title="Qing Dynasty">Manchu Dynasty</a> in China.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1796" title="1796">1796</a>: <a href="/wiki/Trinidad" title="Trinidad">Trinidad</a> becomes British</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1797" title="1797">1797</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Napoleon_I_of_France" title="Napoleon I of France">Napoleon</a>'s invasion and partition of the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Venice" title="Republic of Venice">Republic of Venice</a> ends over 1,000 years of independence for the Serene Republic.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Irish_Rebellion_of_1798" title="Irish Rebellion of 1798">Irish Rebellion</a> fails to overthrow British rule in <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">Ireland</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>–<a href="/wiki/1800" title="1800">1800</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Quasi-War" title="Quasi-War">Quasi-War</a> is fought between the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Napoleon_I_of_France" title="Napoleon I of France">Napoleon</a> stages a <a href="/wiki/Coup_d%27%C3%A9tat" title="Coup d'état">coup d'état</a> and becomes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/First_Consul" title="First Consul">First Consul</a> of <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_India_Company" title="Dutch East India Company">Dutch East India Company</a> is dissolved.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: The assassination of the 14th <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tu%27i_Kanokupolu" title="Tu'i Kanokupolu">Tu'i Kanokupolu</a>, Tukuʻaho, plunges <a href="/wiki/Tonga" title="Tonga">Tonga</a> into half a century of civil war.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: <a href="/wiki/Tipu_Sultan" title="Tipu Sultan">Tipu Sultan</a> is killed in a battle with British forces.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1800"><a href="/wiki/1800" title="1800">1800</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 1800">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1800" title="1800">1800</a>: 1 January, The bankrupt <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_India_Company" title="Dutch East India Company">Dutch East India Company</a> (VOC) is formally dissolved and the nationalised <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_Indies" title="Dutch East Indies">Dutch East Indies</a> are established.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RICKLEFSp106_29-0"><a href="#cite_note-RICKLEFSp106-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Significant_people">Significant people</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Significant people">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="World_leaders,_politicians,_military"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="World_leaders.2C_politicians.2C_military">World leaders, politicians, military</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: World leaders, politicians, military">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<li><a href="/wiki/Black_Caesar_(pirate)" title="Black Caesar (pirate)">Black Caesar</a>, African pirate</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Calico_Jack" title="Calico Jack">Calico Jack</a>, English pirate</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Prosser" title="Gabriel Prosser">Gabriel Prosser</a>, American literate <a href="/wiki/Slavery_in_the_United_States" title="Slavery in the United States">enslaved</a> blacksmith</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Roberts" title="Bartholomew Roberts">Bartholomew Roberts</a>, Welsh pirate</li>
</ul>
<h2><span id="Inventions,_discoveries,_introductions"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Inventions.2C_discoveries.2C_introductions">Inventions, discoveries, introductions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Inventions, discoveries, introductions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Timeline_of_historic_inventions#18th_century" title="Timeline of historic inventions">Timeline of historic inventions § 18th century</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Timeline_of_scientific_discoveries#18th_century" title="Timeline of scientific discoveries">Timeline of scientific discoveries § 18th century</a></div>

The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spinning_Jenny" title="Spinning Jenny">Spinning Jenny</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1330" data-file-width="2224" height="102" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG/170px-Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG/255px-Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG/340px-Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Red_building_Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The Chinese <a href="/wiki/Putuo_Zongcheng_Temple" title="Putuo Zongcheng Temple">Putuo Zongcheng Temple</a> of <a href="/wiki/Chengde" title="Chengde">Chengde</a>, completed in 1771, during the reign of the <a href="/wiki/Qianlong_Emperor" title="Qianlong Emperor">Qianlong Emperor</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1709" title="1709">1709</a>: The first <a href="/wiki/Piano" title="Piano">piano</a> was built by <a href="/wiki/Bartolomeo_Cristofori" title="Bartolomeo Cristofori">Bartolomeo Cristofori</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1711" title="1711">1711</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Tuning_fork" title="Tuning fork">Tuning fork</a> was invented by John Shore</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1712" title="1712">1712</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Steam_engine" title="Steam engine">steam engine</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Newcomen" title="Thomas Newcomen">Thomas Newcomen</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1714" title="1714">1714</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercury_thermometer" title="Mercury thermometer">Mercury thermometer</a> by <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Gabriel_Fahrenheit" title="Daniel Gabriel Fahrenheit">Daniel Gabriel Fahrenheit</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1717" title="1717">1717</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Diving_bell" title="Diving bell">diving bell</a> was successfully tested by <a href="/wiki/Edmond_Halley" title="Edmond Halley">Edmond Halley</a>, sustainable to a depth of 55 ft</li>
<li>c. <a href="/wiki/1730" title="1730">1730</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Octant_(instrument)" title="Octant (instrument)">octant</a> navigational tool was developed by <a href="/wiki/John_Hadley" title="John Hadley">John Hadley</a> in England, and <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Godfrey_(inventor)" title="Thomas Godfrey (inventor)">Thomas Godfrey</a> in <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">America</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1733" title="1733">1733</a>: <a href="/wiki/Flying_shuttle" title="Flying shuttle">Flying shuttle</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/John_Kay_(flying_shuttle)" title="John Kay (flying shuttle)">John Kay</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1736" title="1736">1736</a>: Europeans encountered <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rubber" title="Rubber">rubber</a> – the discovery was made by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles-Marie_de_la_Condamine" title="Charles-Marie de la Condamine">Charles-Marie de la Condamine</a> while on expedition in <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a>. It was named in <a href="/wiki/1770" title="1770">1770</a> by <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Priestley" title="Joseph Priestley">Joseph Priestley</a></li>
<li>c. <a href="/wiki/1740" title="1740">1740</a>: Modern <a href="/wiki/Steel" title="Steel">steel</a> was developed by <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Huntsman" title="Benjamin Huntsman">Benjamin Huntsman</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1741" title="1741">1741</a>: <a href="/wiki/Vitus_Bering" title="Vitus Bering">Vitus Bering</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1745" title="1745">1745</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Leyden_jar" title="Leyden jar">Leyden jar</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Ewald_Georg_von_Kleist" title="Ewald Georg von Kleist">Ewald Georg von Kleist</a> was the first electrical <a href="/wiki/Capacitor" title="Capacitor">capacitor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1752" title="1752">1752</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Lightning_rod" title="Lightning rod">Lightning rod</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Franklin" title="Benjamin Franklin">Benjamin Franklin</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1755" title="1755">1755</a>: The tallest <i>wooden</i> <a href="/wiki/Bodhisattva" title="Bodhisattva">Bodhisattva</a> statue in the world is erected at <a href="/wiki/Puning_Temple" title="Puning Temple">Puning Temple</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chengde" title="Chengde">Chengde</a>, China.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1764" title="1764">1764</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Spinning_jenny" title="Spinning jenny">spinning jenny</a> created by <a href="/wiki/James_Hargreaves" title="James Hargreaves">James Hargreaves</a> brought on the <a href="/wiki/Industrial_Revolution" title="Industrial Revolution">Industrial Revolution</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1765" title="1765">1765</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/James_Watt_(inventor)" title="James Watt (inventor)">James Watt</a> enhances Newcomen's steam engine, allowing new <a href="/wiki/Steel" title="Steel">steel</a> technologies</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1761" title="1761">1761</a>: The problem of <a href="/wiki/Longitude" title="Longitude">Longitude</a> was finally resolved by the fourth <a href="/wiki/Marine_chronometer" title="Marine chronometer">chronometer</a> of <a href="/wiki/John_Harrison" title="John Harrison">John Harrison</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1763" title="1763">1763</a>: <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Bayes" title="Thomas Bayes">Thomas Bayes</a> publishes first version of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bayes%27_Theorem" title="Bayes' Theorem">Bayes' Theorem</a>, paving the way for <a href="/wiki/Bayesian_probability" title="Bayesian probability">Bayesian probability</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1768" title="1768">1768</a>–<a href="/wiki/1779" title="1779">1779</a>: <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a> mapped the boundaries of the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a> and discovered many <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Islands" title="Pacific Islands">Pacific Islands</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1774" title="1774">1774</a>: <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Priestley" title="Joseph Priestley">Joseph Priestley</a> discovers "dephlogisticated air" Oxygen</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1775" title="1775">1775</a>: <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Priestley" title="Joseph Priestley">Joseph Priestley</a> first synthesis of "phlogisticated nitrous air" Nitrous Oxide "laughing gas"</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>: First improved steam engines installed by <a href="/wiki/James_Watt" title="James Watt">James Watt</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Steamboat" title="Steamboat">Steamboat</a> invented by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Claude_de_Jouffroy" title="Claude de Jouffroy">Claude de Jouffroy</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1777" title="1777">1777</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Circular_saw" title="Circular saw">Circular saw</a> invented by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Samuel_Miller_(saw)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Samuel Miller (saw) (page does not exist)">Samuel Miller</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1779" title="1779">1779</a>: <a href="/wiki/Photosynthesis" title="Photosynthesis">Photosynthesis</a> was first discovered by <a href="/wiki/Jan_Ingenhousz" title="Jan Ingenhousz">Jan Ingenhousz</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1781" title="1781">1781</a>: <a href="/wiki/William_Herschel" title="William Herschel">William Herschel</a> announces discovery of Uranus</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1784" title="1784">1784</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Bifocals" title="Bifocals">Bifocals</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Franklin" title="Benjamin Franklin">Benjamin Franklin</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1784" title="1784">1784</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Argand_lamp" title="Argand lamp">Argand lamp</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Aim%C3%A9_Argand" title="Aimé Argand">Aimé Argand</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1785" title="1785">1785</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Power_loom" title="Power loom">Power loom</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Edmund_Cartwright" title="Edmund Cartwright">Edmund Cartwright</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1785" title="1785">1785</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Production_line" title="Production line">Automatic flour mill</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Oliver_Evans" title="Oliver Evans">Oliver Evans</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1786" title="1786">1786</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Threshing_machine" title="Threshing machine">Threshing machine</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Meikle" title="Andrew Meikle">Andrew Meikle</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1787" title="1787">1787</a>: <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Charles" title="Jacques Charles">Jacques Charles</a> discovers <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles%27s_Law" title="Charles's Law">Charles's Law</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: <a href="/wiki/Antoine_Lavoisier" title="Antoine Lavoisier">Antoine Lavoisier</a> discovers the law of conservation of mass, the basis for chemistry, and begins modern chemistry</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>: <a href="/wiki/Edward_Jenner" title="Edward Jenner">Edward Jenner</a> publishes a treatise about <a href="/wiki/Smallpox" title="Smallpox">smallpox</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vaccination" title="Vaccination">vaccination</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Lithography" title="Lithography">Lithographic printing process</a> invented by <a href="/wiki/Alois_Senefelder" title="Alois Senefelder">Alois Senefelder</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1799" title="1799">1799</a>: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rosetta_stone" title="Rosetta stone">Rosetta stone</a> discovered by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Napoleon_I_of_France" title="Napoleon I of France">Napoleon</a>'s troops</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Literary_and_philosophical_achievements">Literary and philosophical achievements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Literary and philosophical achievements">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1703" title="1703">1703</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Love_Suicides_at_Sonezaki" title="The Love Suicides at Sonezaki">The Love Suicides at Sonezaki</a></i> by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chikamatsu" title="Chikamatsu">Chikamatsu</a> first performed</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1704" title="1704">1704</a>–<a href="/wiki/1717" title="1717">1717</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/One_Thousand_and_One_Nights" title="One Thousand and One Nights">One Thousand and One Nights</a></i> translated into French by <a href="/wiki/Antoine_Galland" title="Antoine Galland">Antoine Galland</a>. The work becomes immensely popular throughout Europe.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1704" title="1704">1704</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/A_Tale_of_a_Tub" title="A Tale of a Tub">A Tale of a Tub</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Swift" title="Jonathan Swift">Jonathan Swift</a> first published</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1712" title="1712">1712</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Rape_of_the_Lock" title="The Rape of the Lock">The Rape of the Lock</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Pope" title="Alexander Pope">Alexander Pope</a> (publication of first version)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1719" title="1719">1719</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Robinson_Crusoe" title="Robinson Crusoe">Robinson Crusoe</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Defoe" title="Daniel Defoe">Daniel Defoe</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1725" title="1725">1725</a>: <i>The New Science</i> by <a href="/wiki/Giambattista_Vico" title="Giambattista Vico">Giambattista Vico</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1726" title="1726">1726</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Gulliver%27s_Travels" title="Gulliver's Travels">Gulliver's Travels</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Swift" title="Jonathan Swift">Jonathan Swift</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1728" title="1728">1728</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Dunciad" title="The Dunciad">The Dunciad</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Pope" title="Alexander Pope">Alexander Pope</a> (publication of first version)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1744" title="1744">1744</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/A_Little_Pretty_Pocket-Book" title="A Little Pretty Pocket-Book">A Little Pretty Pocket-Book</a></i> becomes one of the first <a href="/wiki/Children%27s_literature#History" title="Children's literature">books marketed for children</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1748" title="1748">1748</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chushingura" title="Chushingura">Chushingura</a></i> (<i>The Treasury of Loyal Retainers</i>), popular Japanese <a href="/wiki/Bunraku" title="Bunraku">puppet play</a>, composed</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1748" title="1748">1748</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Clarissa" title="Clarissa">Clarissa</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Richardson" title="Samuel Richardson">Samuel Richardson</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1749" title="1749">1749</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_History_of_Tom_Jones,_a_Foundling" title="The History of Tom Jones, a Foundling">The History of Tom Jones, a Foundling</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Henry_Fielding" title="Henry Fielding">Henry Fielding</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1751" title="1751">1751</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Elegy_Written_in_a_Country_Churchyard" title="Elegy Written in a Country Churchyard">Elegy Written in a Country Churchyard</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Gray" title="Thomas Gray">Thomas Gray</a> published</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1751" title="1751">1751</a>–<a href="/wiki/1785" title="1785">1785</a>: The French <a href="/wiki/Encyclop%C3%A9die" title="Encyclopédie">Encyclopédie</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1755" title="1755">1755</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/A_Dictionary_of_the_English_Language" title="A Dictionary of the English Language">A Dictionary of the English Language</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Johnson" title="Samuel Johnson">Samuel Johnson</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1759" title="1759">1759</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Candide" title="Candide">Candide</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Voltaire" title="Voltaire">Voltaire</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1759" title="1759">1759</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Theory_of_Moral_Sentiments" title="The Theory of Moral Sentiments">The Theory of Moral Sentiments</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Adam_Smith" title="Adam Smith">Adam Smith</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1759" title="1759">1759</a>–<a href="/wiki/1767" title="1767">1767</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tristram_Shandy" title="Tristram Shandy">Tristram Shandy</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Laurence_Sterne" title="Laurence Sterne">Laurence Sterne</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1762" title="1762">1762</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Emile:_or,_On_Education" title="Emile: or, On Education">Emile: or, On Education</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Jean-Jacques_Rousseau" title="Jean-Jacques Rousseau">Jean-Jacques Rousseau</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1762" title="1762">1762</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Social_Contract_(Rousseau)" title="Social Contract (Rousseau)">The Social Contract, Or Principles of Political Right</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Jean-Jacques_Rousseau" title="Jean-Jacques Rousseau">Jean-Jacques Rousseau</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1774" title="1774">1774</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sorrows_of_Young_Werther" title="The Sorrows of Young Werther">The Sorrows of Young Werther</a></i> by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Goethe" title="Goethe">Goethe</a> first published</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Ugetsu_Monogatari" title="Ugetsu Monogatari">Ugetsu Monogatari</a></i> (<i>Tales of Moonlight and Rain</i>) by <a href="/wiki/Ueda_Akinari" title="Ueda Akinari">Ueda Akinari</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wealth_of_Nations" title="The Wealth of Nations">The Wealth of Nations</a></i>, foundation of the modern theory of economy, was published by <a href="/wiki/Adam_Smith" title="Adam Smith">Adam Smith</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1776" title="1776">1776</a>–<a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_History_of_the_Decline_and_Fall_of_the_Roman_Empire" title="The History of the Decline and Fall of the Roman Empire">The History of the Decline and Fall of the Roman Empire</a></i> was published by <a href="/wiki/Edward_Gibbon" title="Edward Gibbon">Edward Gibbon</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1779" title="1779">1779</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Amazing_Grace" title="Amazing Grace">Amazing Grace</a></i> published by <a href="/wiki/John_Newton" title="John Newton">John Newton</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1779" title="1779">1779</a>–<a href="/wiki/1782" title="1782">1782</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Lives_of_the_Most_Eminent_English_Poets" title="Lives of the Most Eminent English Poets">Lives of the Most Eminent English Poets</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Johnson" title="Samuel Johnson">Samuel Johnson</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1781" title="1781">1781</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Critique_of_Pure_Reason" title="Critique of Pure Reason">Critique of Pure Reason</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Immanuel_Kant" title="Immanuel Kant">Immanuel Kant</a> (publication of first edition)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1781" title="1781">1781</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Robbers" title="The Robbers">The Robbers</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Friedrich_Schiller" title="Friedrich Schiller">Friedrich Schiller</a> first published</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1782" title="1782">1782</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Les_Liaisons_dangereuses" title="Les Liaisons dangereuses">Les Liaisons dangereuses</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Choderlos_de_Laclos" title="Pierre Choderlos de Laclos">Pierre Choderlos de Laclos</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1786" title="1786">1786</a>: <i>Poems, Chiefly in the Scottish Dialect</i> by <a href="/wiki/Robert_Burns" title="Robert Burns">Robert Burns</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1787" title="1787">1787</a>–<a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Federalist_Papers" title="The Federalist Papers">The Federalist Papers</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Hamilton" title="Alexander Hamilton">Alexander Hamilton</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Madison" title="James Madison">James Madison</a>, and <a href="/wiki/John_Jay" title="John Jay">John Jay</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Critique_of_Practical_Reason" title="Critique of Practical Reason">Critique of Practical Reason</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Immanuel_Kant" title="Immanuel Kant">Immanuel Kant</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1789" title="1789">1789</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Songs_of_Innocence" title="Songs of Innocence">Songs of Innocence</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/William_Blake" title="William Blake">William Blake</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1790" title="1790">1790</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Journey_from_St._Petersburg_to_Moscow" title="Journey from St. Petersburg to Moscow">Journey from St. Petersburg to Moscow</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Radishchev" title="Alexander Radishchev">Alexander Radishchev</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1790" title="1790">1790</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Reflections_on_the_Revolution_in_France" title="Reflections on the Revolution in France">Reflections on the Revolution in France</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Edmund_Burke" title="Edmund Burke">Edmund Burke</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Rights_of_Man" title="Rights of Man">Rights of Man</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Paine" title="Thomas Paine">Thomas Paine</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1792" title="1792">1792</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vindication_of_the_Rights_of_Women" title="Vindication of the Rights of Women">Vindication of the Rights of Women</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Mary_Wollstonecraft" title="Mary Wollstonecraft">Mary Wollstonecraft</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1794" title="1794">1794</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Songs_of_Experience" title="Songs of Experience">Songs of Experience</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/William_Blake" title="William Blake">William Blake</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Lyrical_Ballads" title="Lyrical Ballads">Lyrical Ballads</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/William_Wordsworth" title="William Wordsworth">William Wordsworth</a> and <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Taylor_Coleridge" title="Samuel Taylor Coleridge">Samuel Taylor Coleridge</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/An_Essay_on_the_Principle_of_Population" title="An Essay on the Principle of Population">An Essay on the Principle of Population</a></i> published by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thomas_Malthus" title="Thomas Malthus">Thomas Malthus</a></li>
<li>(mid-18th century): <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Dream_of_the_Red_Chamber" title="The Dream of the Red Chamber">The Dream of the Red Chamber</a></i> (authorship attributed to <a href="/wiki/Cao_Xueqin" title="Cao Xueqin">Cao Xueqin</a>), one of the most famous Chinese novels</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Musical_works">Musical works</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=18th_century&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Musical works">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1711" title="1711">1711</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Rinaldo_(opera)" title="Rinaldo (opera)">Rinaldo</a></i>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Handel" title="Handel">Handel</a>'s first opera for the London stage, premiered</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1721" title="1721">1721</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brandenburg_concertos" title="Brandenburg concertos">Brandenburg concertos</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Johann_Sebastian_Bach" title="Johann Sebastian Bach">J.S. Bach</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1723" title="1723">1723</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Four_Seasons_(Vivaldi)" title="The Four Seasons (Vivaldi)">The Four Seasons</a></i>, violin concertos by <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Vivaldi" title="Antonio Vivaldi">Antonio Vivaldi</a>, composed</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1724" title="1724">1724</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Johannes_Passion" title="Johannes Passion">St John Passion</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Johann_Sebastian_Bach" title="Johann Sebastian Bach">J.S. Bach</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1727" title="1727">1727</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St_Matthew_Passion_(Bach)" title="St Matthew Passion (Bach)">St Matthew Passion</a></i> composed by <a href="/wiki/Johann_Sebastian_Bach" title="Johann Sebastian Bach">J.S. Bach</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1733" title="1733">1733</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Hippolyte_et_Aricie" title="Hippolyte et Aricie">Hippolyte et Aricie</a></i>, first opera by <a href="/wiki/Jean-Philippe_Rameau" title="Jean-Philippe Rameau">Jean-Philippe Rameau</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1741" title="1741">1741</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Goldberg_Variations" title="Goldberg Variations">Goldberg Variations</a></i> for <a href="/wiki/Harpsichord" title="Harpsichord">harpsichord</a> published by <a href="/wiki/Johann_Sebastian_Bach" title="Johann Sebastian Bach">Bach</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1742" title="1742">1742</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Messiah_(Handel)" title="Messiah (Handel)">Messiah</a></i>, oratorio by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Handel" title="Handel">Handel</a> premiered in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1749" title="1749">1749</a>: <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mass_in_B_Minor" title="Mass in B Minor">Mass in B Minor</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Johann_Sebastian_Bach" title="Johann Sebastian Bach">J.S. Bach</a> assembled in current form</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1751" title="1751">1751</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Art_of_Fugue" title="The Art of Fugue">The Art of Fugue</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Johann_Sebastian_Bach" title="Johann Sebastian Bach">J.S. Bach</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1762" title="1762">1762</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Orfeo_ed_Euridice" title="Orfeo ed Euridice">Orfeo ed Euridice</a></i>, first "reform opera" by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Christoph_Willibald_von_Gluck" title="Christoph Willibald von Gluck">Gluck</a>, performed in <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1786" title="1786">1786</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Marriage_of_Figaro" title="The Marriage of Figaro">The Marriage of Figaro</a></i>, opera by <a href="/wiki/Wolfgang_Amadeus_Mozart" title="Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart">Mozart</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1787" title="1787">1787</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Don_Giovanni" title="Don Giovanni">Don Giovanni</a></i>, opera by <a href="/wiki/Wolfgang_Amadeus_Mozart" title="Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart">Mozart</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1788" title="1788">1788</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Symphony_No._41_(Mozart)" title="Symphony No. 41 (Mozart)">Jupiter Symphony</a> (Symphony No.41)</i> composed by <a href="/wiki/Wolfgang_Amadeus_Mozart" title="Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart">Mozart</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Magic_Flute" title="The Magic Flute">The Magic Flute</a></i>, opera by <a href="/wiki/Wolfgang_Amadeus_Mozart" title="Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart">Mozart</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1791" title="1791">1791</a>–<a href="/wiki/1795" title="1795">1795</a>: <a href="/wiki/London_symphonies" title="London symphonies">London symphonies</a> by <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Haydn" title="Joseph Haydn">Haydn</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Piano_Sonata_No._8_(Beethoven)" title="Piano Sonata No. 8 (Beethoven)">Pathétique,</a> piano sonata by <a href="/wiki/Ludwig_van_Beethoven" title="Ludwig van Beethoven">Beethoven</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/1798" title="1798">1798</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Creation_(Haydn)" title="The Creation (Haydn)">The Creation</a></i>, oratorio by <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Haydn" title="Joseph Haydn">Haydn</a> first performed</li>
</ul>

Refereed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wallace_Collection" title="Wallace Collection">The Wallace Collection</a>, London, houses one of the finest collections of 18th-century decorative arts from France, England and Italy, including paintings, furniture, porcelain and gold boxes.</li>
